  <script type="application/javascript">
   /**
 * Test, if current url starts, ends, is or contain $requested url
 */
function isExpectedUrl($type, $requested, $current) {
    switch($type) {
        case 'start':
            return ($current.slice(0, $requested.length) == $requested);

        case 'end':
            return ($current.indexOf($requested, $current.length - $requested.length) !== -1);

        case 'is':
            return ($requested === $current) ? true : false;

        case 'contain':
            return ($current.indexOf($requested) != -1) ? true : false;
    }

    return false;
}

$(document).ready(function() {
    var $url = window.location.pathname;

});
  </script>

   $(document).ready(function() {
    // for snippet/simulator_box.latte
    $('.simForm').submit(function() {
        var loginStatus = $("#login-data").attr("data-status");

        if ((loginStatus != "connected") && ($('#spiny').val() > 500)) {
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            notice.message = "Simulaci pro více než 500 spinů můžete provést až po přihlásení.";
            notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Warning;
            notice.open();

            return false;
        }
    });
});

  <script>
   (function(d, s, id) {
var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/cs_CZ/sdk.js#xfbml=1&version=v2.3";
fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
}(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));

window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
    FB.init({
      appId      : 1420149944957455,
      xfbml      : true,
      cookie     : true,
      version    : 'v2.3'
    });

    FB.getLoginStatus(function(response){
        //console.log(response);
        if (response.status == 'connected') {
            $("#login-data").attr("data-status", "connected");
            $("#login-data").attr("data-type", "facebook");

            FB.api('/me', function(response) {
                $("#login-data").attr("data-userId", response.id);
                $("#login-data").attr("data-name", response.name);
                //console.log(JSON.stringify(response));
                updateLogin();
            });
        }
    });
 };

function facebookLogin() {
    FB.login(function(response) {
        $.fancybox.close();
        if (response.status !== 'connected') {
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            notice.message = "Přihlášení selhalo.";
            notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Warning;
            notice.open();
        } else {
            FB.api('/me', function(response) {
                loginApp('facebook', response.id, response.name, function(){
                    window.location = getUrl();
                });
            });
        }
    });
}
  </script>

      // tabs
var tabber1 = new Yetii({
id: 'tab-boxes3',
active: 1,
tabclass: 'tab-box3',
activeclass: 'active'
});

$(document).ready(function() {
    // slide big game with images
    var setup = 0;
    var clonsCount2 = 4; // pocet zobrazenych prvkov
    var boxCount_origin2 = $(".flg ul li").size();
    var minus2 = boxCount_origin2 - 1;
    $(".flg ul").css('marginLeft', -boxCount_origin2 * 122  + 'px');
    var marg;
    for (i=0; i<clonsCount2; i++) {
        $('.flg ul li:eq('+i+')').clone().insertAfter($('.flg ul li:eq(' + minus2 + ')'));
        minus2++;
    }
    var minus2 = boxCount_origin2 - 1;
    for (i=0; i<boxCount_origin2; i++) {
        $('.flg ul li:eq(' + minus2 + ')').clone().insertBefore($('.flg ul li:eq(0)'));
    }
    $('.arrwleft').click(function(){
        setup++;
        marg = setup * ($('.flg ul li').width() + 11) - (boxCount_origin2 * 122);
        $(".flg ul").animate({ marginLeft: marg + 'px'}, 200);
        if(setup==boxCount_origin2){
                $(".flg ul").animate({ marginLeft: marg + 'px'}, 200, function(){ $(".flg ul").css('marginLeft', -boxCount_origin2 * 122  + 'px');return false;});
                setup = 0;
        }
        return false;
    });
    $('.arrwright').click(function(){
        setup--;
        marg = setup * ($('.flg ul li').width() + 11) - (boxCount_origin2 * 122);
        //$(".flg ul").css('marginLeft', marg + 'px');
        $(".flg ul").animate({ marginLeft: marg + 'px'}, 200);
        if(setup==-boxCount_origin2){
                //$(".flg ul").css('marginLeft', -boxCount_origin2 * 160  + 'px');
                $(".flg ul").animate({ marginLeft: marg + 'px'}, 200, function(){ $(".flg ul").css('marginLeft', -boxCount_origin2 * 122  + 'px');return false;});
                setup = 0;
        }
        return false;
    });

    // slide game list
    $('.katies div:eq(5), .katies div:eq(10)').addClass('clearleft');
    $('.forgic').each(function(){
        kolkoLi = $(this).find('li').size();
        kolkoStranok = ((kolkoLi - kolkoLi%15)/15);
        kolkoStranok++;
        $(this).find('.forgis').css('width', 456 * kolkoStranok + "px");

        if(kolkoStranok>1){
            $(this).addClass('tsst');
            $(this).append('<ul class="rttit"></ul>');
            for(i=0;i<kolkoStranok;i++){
                    $(this).children('.rttit').append('<li><a href="" class="pgt' + i + '" rel="' + i + '"></a></li>');
            }
            $(this).find('.rttit li:first').children('a').addClass('active');
        }
    });
    $('.rttit a').click(function(){
        if(!$(this).hasClass('active')){
            tptpk = parseInt($(this).attr('rel'));
            tptpk2 = (-1) * (tptpk) * 456 + "px";
            $(this).parent('li').parent('.rttit').parent('.forgic').find('.forgis').stop(true, true).animate({ marginLeft: tptpk2}, 300);

            $(this).parent('li').siblings('li').children('a').removeClass('active');
            $(this).addClass('active');
        }
        return false;
    });
});

       <script>
        $(document).ready(function() {
    $("#frm-searchForm-submit").click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var query = encodeURIComponent($("#frm-searchForm-query").val());
        var url = $("#frm-searchForm-query").attr("data-submit-url");

        if (query.length == 0) {
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            notice.message = "Zadejte, prosím, hledaný výraz.";
            notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Warning;
            notice.open();

            return false;
        }

        if (url.indexOf("?") != -1) {
            // there are params
            window.location = url + '&query=' + query;
        } else {
            window.location = url + '?query=' + query;
        }

    });

    // submit with enter key
    $("#frm-searchForm-query").keyup(function(event){
        if(event.keyCode == 13 /* enter */) {
            $("#frm-searchForm-submit").click();
        }
    });
});
       </script>

       <script>
        $(document).ready(function() {
    // @overwrite
    Nette.addError = function(elem, message) {
        if (elem.focus) {
            elem.focus();
        }
        if (message) {
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            notice.message = message;
            notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Warning;
            notice.open();
        }
    };

    $('#frm-newsletterForm').submit(function(e){
        e.preventDefault();

        if (!Nette.validateForm(this))
            return false;

        $.post($(this).attr("action"), $(this).serialize(), function(data){
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            if (typeof data.status == 'undefined') {
                notice.message = "Neznámá chyba. Načtěte stránku znovu a akci, prosím, opakujte.";
                notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Error;
            } else {
                notice.message = data.message;
                notice.severity = (data.status) ? ICasina.MessageSeverity.Success : ICasina.MessageSeverity.Warning;
            }
            notice.open();

        }).fail(function(){
            var notice = new ICasina.Notice();
            notice.message = "Neznámá chyba. Načtěte stránku znovu a akci, prosím, opakujte.";
            notice.severity = ICasina.MessageSeverity.Error;
            notice.open();
        });

        return false;
    });
});
       </script>
